<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Aura_effect">Aura effect</span></h3>
<div style="max-width: 100%; overflow-x: auto;">
<table class="wikitable sortable modifier-table jquery-tablesorter" style="max-width: 100%;">
<thead>
    <tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Curse_effect">Curse effect</span></h3>
<div style="max-width: 100%; overflow-x: auto;">
<table class="wikitable sortable modifier-table jquery-tablesorter" style="max-width: 100%;">
<thead>
    <tr>
        <th data-sort-type="text" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"
            title="Sort ascending"><abbr
                title="Name of the modifier if available or its internal identifier instead"
                class="">Name</abbr></th>
        <th data-sort-type="number" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"
            title="Sort ascending"><img
                alt="For generated item/monster modifiers the minimum item/monster level respectively. Some generation types may not require this condition to be met, however item level restrictions may be raised to 80% of this value."
                src="https://gamepedia.cursecdn.com/pathofexile_gamepedia/d/d1/Level_up_icon_small.png?version=4724312c4874bedd02f533b5e61fb331"
                decoding="async"
                title="For generated item/monster modifiers the minimum item/monster level respectively. Some generation types may not require this condition to be met, however item level restrictions may be raised to 80% of this value."
                width="22" height="22"></th>
        <th data-sort-type="text" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"

                title="Stats of the modifier and the range they can roll in (if applicable)"
                class="">Stats</abbr></th>
        <th data-sort-type="text" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"

        <th class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button" title="Sort ascending">weight</th>
    </tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Critical_strike_chance">Critical strike chance</span></h3>
<div style="max-width: 100%; overflow-x: auto;">
<table class="wikitable sortable modifier-table jquery-tablesorter" style="max-width: 100%;">
<thead>
    <tr>
        <th data-sort-type="text" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"
            title="Sort ascending"><abbr
                title="Name of the modifier if available or its internal identifier instead"
                class="">Name</abbr></th>
        <th data-sort-type="number" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"
            title="Sort ascending"><img
                alt="For generated item/monster modifiers the minimum item/monster level respectively. Some generation types may not require this condition to be met, however item level restrictions may be raised to 80% of this value."
                src="https://gamepedia.cursecdn.com/pathofexile_gamepedia/d/d1/Level_up_icon_small.png?version=4724312c4874bedd02f533b5e61fb331"
                decoding="async"
                title="For generated item/monster modifiers the minimum item/monster level respectively. Some generation types may not require this condition to be met, however item level restrictions may be raised to 80% of this value."
                width="22" height="22"></th>
        <th data-sort-type="text" class="headerSort" tabindex="0" role="columnheader button"
            title="Sort ascending"><abbr
                title="Stats of the modifier and the range they can roll in (if applicable)"
                class="">Stats</abbr></th>
